texlive-tex4ht in Fedora 34

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of texlive-tex4ht. You might want go back to the main page of texlive-tex4ht.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-02-02 Tom Callaway - 7:20200327-28 - set TEXMFLOCAL during the context scriptlet to minimize the scope of where it looks during mtxrun --generate
2021-01-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 9:20200327-27 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_34_Mass_Rebuild
2021-01-26 Tomas Popela - 9:20200327-26 - Don't build texlive-xindy on ELN because of its requirements (clisp)
2021-01-15 Tom Callaway - 9:20200327-25 - debootstrap
2021-01-15 Tom Callaway - 9:20200327-24 - fix context shell binary to handle /home dirs that are symlinks (bz1913245)
2020-12-30 Tom Callaway - 9:20200327-23 - update pygmentex (supports python3) - update dviasm (supports python3)
2020-11-16 Tom Callaway - 9:20200327-22 - make proper texlive-optex subpackage by moving it here - bump epoch to 9 so this texlive-optex package replaces the one that used to live in texlive
2020-11-12 Tom Callaway - 7:20200327-21 - obsolete texlive-texconfig, texlive-pdftools, texlive-pstools (in texlive-texlive-scripts-extra)
2020-11-10 Tom Callaway - 7:20200327-20 - fix issues with file ownership duplication - fix issue with obsoleting texlive-tetex - turn LTO back off, as it was assuming code needed libcrypto for some unknown reason
2020-10-29 Tom Callaway - 7:20200327-19 - fix dependencies of texlive-ptex and texlive-uptex
